    Euler_Angle_Order Â¶
    Source

    Euler_Angle_Order :: enum int {
	// Tait-Bryan
	XYZ, 
	XZY, 
	YXZ, 
	YZX, 
	ZXY, 
	ZYX, 
	// Proper Euler
	XYX, 
	XZX, 
	YXY, 
	YZY, 
	ZXZ, 
	ZYZ, 
}
